  <h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Muralize Privacy Policy</h2><h4 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Last updated: October 31, 2016</h4><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Magnopus ("us", "we", or "our") has created "Muralize", an Application built for the Microsoft HoloLens.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">This page informs you of our policies regarding the collection, use and disclosure of Personal Information we receive from users of the Application.</p><p class="" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>OUR POLICY IS SIMPLE: MURALIZE DOES NOT COLLECT OR TRANSMIT YOUR INFORMATION TO MAGNOPUS.</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>THE INFORMATION YOU ENTER WILL BE USED ONLY TO CREATE WEB-QUERIES IN REAL TIME.</strong></p><p class="" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"></p><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Changes To This Privacy Policy:</h3><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">This Privacy Policy is effective as of October 31, 2016 and will remain in effect except with respect to any changes in its provisions in the future, which will be in effect immediately after being posted on this page.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We reserve the right to update or change our Privacy Policy at any time and you should check this Privacy Policy periodically. Your continued use of the Service after we post any modifications to the Privacy Policy on this page will constitute your acknowledgment of the modifications and your consent to abide and be bound by the modified Privacy Policy.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">If we make any material changes to this Privacy Policy, we will notify you by placing a prominent notice on our Application page in the Microsoft App Store.</p><p class="" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"></p><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">INSTAGRAM PRIVACY POLICY</h3><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">As we use Instagram to query your photos, if you have any questions about the Instagram Privacy Policy, please go here.</p><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"> </h3><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">PLEASE CONTACT US</h3><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">If you have any questions about this Privacy Policy, please <a href="/contact">contact us</a>.</p>

            sectionBackground.style.top = headerHeight + 'px';
          } else {
            sectionBackground.style.top = '';
          }

<script>
   window.onscroll = function() {scrollFunction()};

   function scrollFunction() {
     var myBtn = document.getElementById("myBtn");
     
      if (document.body.scrollTop > 20 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 20)
      {
        myBtn.classList.add("btnActive");
      } else {
         myBtn.classList.remove("btnActive");
      }
   }

   function topFunction() {
      $('html,body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 1000);
   }
</script>
